<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>VALEANT PHARMACEUTICALS REPORTS SECOND QUARTER 2015 FINANCIAL RESULTS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>2015 Second Quarter Results </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Total Revenue $2.7 billion</B><B>; an increase of 34% over the prior year</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="9%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Excluding negative impact of foreign exchange ($173 million) and the contribution of Salix ($313 million), revenue increased 27% over the prior year</B> </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Same Store Sales Organic Growth was 19%, driven by:</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="9%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Cash EPS $3.98 - $4.18 per share</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Laval, Quebec </B>&#151; July&nbsp;23, 2015 &#151;
Valeant Pharmaceuticals International, Inc. (NYSE: VRX) (TSX: VRX) announces second quarter financial results for 2015. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We once
again exceeded our guidance and delivered our fourth consecutive quarter of greater than 15% organic growth,&#148; stated J. Michael Pearson, chairman and chief executive officer. &#147;Our strong second quarter results were driven by outperformance
in our U.S. businesses, strong results in certain emerging markets and outstanding starts to both the Salix and Dendreon acquisitions. In addition, we have signed eight new transactions so far this year and have realized several significant R&amp;D
milestones, including the approval of Xifaxan for IBS-D and the NDA submissions for Vesneo and Relistor Oral. As a result, we feel confident in raising our guidance for the remainder of 2015.&#148; </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Valeant </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Valeant Pharmaceuticals
International, Inc. (NYSE/TSX:VRX) is a multinational specialty pharmaceutical company that develops, manufactures and markets a broad range of pharmaceutical products primarily in the areas of dermatology, gastrointestinal disorder, eye health,
neurology and branded generics. More information about Valeant can be found at <U>www.valeant.com</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Forward-looking Statements </B></P>

</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Non-GAAP Information </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">To supplement the financial
measures prepared in accordance with U.S. generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP), the company uses non-GAAP financial measures that exclude certain items, such as amortization of inventory step-up, amortization of alliance product
assets&nbsp;&amp; property, plant and equipment step up, stock-based compensation step-up, contingent consideration fair value adjustments, restructuring, integration, acquisition-related and other costs, In-process research and development,
impairments and other charges, (&#147;IPR&amp;D&#148;), legal settlements outside the ordinary course of business, the impact of currency fluctuations, amortization including intangible asset impairments and other non-cash charges, amortization and
write-down of deferred financing costs, debt discounts and ASC 470-20 (FSP APB 14-1) interest, loss on extinguishment of debt, (gain) loss on assets sold/held for sale/impairment, net, (gain) loss on investments, net, and adjusts tax expense to cash
taxes. Management uses non-GAAP financial measures internally for strategic decision making, forecasting future results and evaluating current performance. By disclosing non-GAAP financial measures, management intends to provide investors with a
meaningful, consistent comparison of the company&#146;s core operating results and trends for the periods presented. Non-GAAP financial measures are not prepared in accordance with GAAP. </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">To supplement the financial measures prepared in accordance with U.S. generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP), the company uses non-GAAP financial measures that exclude certain items, such as amortization of
inventory step-up, amortization of alliance product assets&nbsp;&amp; property, plant and equipment step-up, stock-based compensation step-up, contingent consideration fair value adjustments, restructuring, integration, acquisition-related and other
costs, In-process research and development, impairments and other charges, (&#147;IPR&amp;D&#148;), legal settlements outside the ordinary course of business, the impact of currency fluctuations, amortization including intangible asset impairments
and other non-cash charges, amortization and write-down of deferred financing costs, debt discounts and ASC 470-20 (FSP APB 14-1) interest, loss on extinguishment of debt, (gain) loss on assets sold/held for sale/impairment, net, (gain) loss on
investments, net, and adjusts tax expense to cash taxes. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management uses non-GAAP financial measures internally for
strategic decision making, forecasting future results and evaluating current performance. By disclosing non-GAAP financial measures, management intends to provide investors with a meaningful, consistent comparison of the company&#146;s core
operating results and trends for the periods presented. Non-GAAP financial measures are not prepared in accordance with GAAP. Therefore, the information is not necessarily comparable to other companies and should be considered as a supplement to,
not a substitute for, or superior to, the corresponding measures calculated in accordance with GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">To supplement the financial measures prepared in accordance with U.S. generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP), the company uses non-GAAP financial measures that exclude certain items, such as amortization of
inventory step-up, amortization of alliance product assets&nbsp;&amp; property, plant and equipment step-up, stock-based compensation step-up, contingent consideration fair value adjustments, restructuring, integration, acquisition-related and other
costs, In-process research and development, impairments and other charges, (&#147;IPR&amp;D&#148;), legal settlements outside the ordinary course of business, the impact of currency fluctuations, amortization including intangible asset impairments
and other non-cash charges, amortization and write-down of deferred financing costs, debt discounts and ASC 470-20 (FSP APB 14-1) interest, loss on extinguishment of debt, (gain) loss on assets sold/held for sale/impairment, net, (gain) loss on
investments, net, and adjusts tax expense to cash taxes. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management uses non-GAAP financial measures internally for
strategic decision making, forecasting future results and evaluating current performance. By disclosing non-GAAP financial measures, management intends to provide investors with a meaningful, consistent comparison of the company&#146;s core
operating results and trends for the periods presented. Non-GAAP financial measures are not prepared in accordance with GAAP. Therefore, the information is not necessarily comparable to other companies and should be considered as a supplement to,
not a substitute for, or superior to, the corresponding measures calculated in accordance with GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">ASC 805, Business Combinations, requires an inventory fair value step-up whose total impact for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 is $70.5 million primarily due to the acquisitions of Marathon Pharmaceuticals, LLC
on February&nbsp;10, 2015 and Salix Pharmaceuticals Ltd on April&nbsp;1, 2015 . For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014 the impact of inventory fair value step-up is $9.6 million primarily due to the acquisition of Solta Medical, Inc. on
January&nbsp;23, 2014. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(c)</TD>

million and $10.1 million, respectively, primarily relating to the acquisition of Bausch&nbsp;&amp; Lomb Holdings Incorporated. For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014, cost of goods sold also includes $3.0 million amortization of a BMS fair
value inventory adjustment. </TD></TR></TABLE>

includes $4.3 million of stock-based compensation which reflects acceleration of certain equity instruments and registration fees associated with the proposed Allergan transaction, $6.2 million. </TD></TR></TABLE>

&#150; divestitures&nbsp;&amp; discontinuations))/(Prior Year Total product sales &#150; divestitures&nbsp;&amp; discontinuations) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pro Forma (PF): This
measure provides year over year growth rates for the entire business, including those that have been acquired within the last year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">((Current Year Total
product sales + YoY FX impact) &#150; (Prior Year Total product sales + Pro Forma impact of acquisitions within the last year - divestitures or discontinuations))/(Prior Year Total product sales + Pro Forma impact of acquisitions within the last
year - divestitures or discontinuations). </P>
